posted:Posted April 6, 2024
msg:Shanghai Accommodation ~ Fairytale Castle in the City Center

Shanghai has many European-style buildings. I personally think that you must experience living in a historical site once in your life. After all, the opportunity is rare. Villa Mahler is a 90-year-old garden villa that combines European and Asian styles. It has also been authoritatively rated as one of the "Ten Most Classic Works of Architectural Design in the 20th Century" by the European Architects and Design Association. This is the most expensive hotel in the entire trip, and it‚Äôs also the most check-in hotel. I don‚Äôt want to check out at all.

üöáTransportation: Take Metro Line 1 to Nanjing West Road Station, Exit 12, and walk for about ten minutes.

ü§µüèªService: There were welcome snacks and fruits when we checked in, but we arrived too late and didn't enjoy them. When leaving, the staff also gave two packs of handmade biscuits and villa-shaped magnets to each room guest. If there were children, toys were given as well, which was really thoughtful.

üèõÔ∏èEnvironment: There are two main buildings, namely Building 1, which is mainly a hotel room and a restaurant building in No. 2. There are two outdoor gardens, one is near the restaurant with a large green lawn, and the other is a maze on the periphery. type lawn. The exterior is a three-story Nordic Gothic architectural style, with Norwegian spires and Gothic spires. The exterior walls are made of ocher yellow refractory bricks. The interior is mainly made of wood, with heavy-weight mahogany tables, chairs, and candlesticks. With palace-style crystal chandeliers, stained glass on the indoor dome, Chinese glazed tiles, and many exquisite Chinese porcelain plate decorations, the design theme of combining Chinese and Western elements creates a picturesque scenery in Shanghai!

üè†Room: Superior King Room HK$1,397.04/one night + buffet breakfast (original price)
The package includes free Minibar drinks, one tour of the castle (starting at 10 o'clock every day) and exquisite gifts. I was a little disappointed with the tour of the castle because there are not many facilities to visit, and the second and third floors are not open, which is a bit small. disappoin**ent.

The area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe room is not very large, but the bathroom feels larger. The main color is green marble, which is very fresh and natural, but there is no place to hang clothes, which is a fly in the oin**ent. The interior decoration is mainly in palace style and has complete facilities, but it feels cramped because the dressing table in the middle is too big and separates the big bed and the entrance area, making the room feel cramped.

msg:If you want to experience the old Shanghai style in Shanghai, staying at Mahler Villa Hotel is the best choice. The hotel is located at No. 30, Shaanxi South Road, Jing'an District. It was built in the 25th year of the Republic of China (1936) and is a Nordic Norwegian-style building built by the British Jewish businessman Eric Mahler. The ancient building has modern facilities and is clean and hygienic. The windows are equipped with double-layer soundproof glass, and the room is very quiet. The service is thoughtful, and there are waiters to carry luggage in and out. The buffet breakfast has a variety of styles, combining Chinese and Western. It is convenient to travel. There is a bus stop at the door of the hotel, and the stations of many subway lines such as 2, 8, 10, 12, 13, and 14 are all within 1 kilometer. The price is affordable and the cost performance is very high!

The sunlight is projecting in through the colored windows, and suddenly there is a sense of solemnity of the church in a trance.
Visit the villa. The building is very quiet, with almost no people. It is as large as the living room, lounge, and terrace, as small as the stairway, on the stairs, and at every corner. There are scenery everywhere, and beautiful pictures can be seen everywhere. It can be seen that the design of the hotel is very careful. The level of the designer is high. Building No. 1 and Building No. 2 are connected internally. Although there are only three floors, there are many corridors and curves inside. It is a bit confusing to turn around in the two small conjoined buildings. No wonder some residents said that there will be get lost. Most of the stairs, floors, and wall panels are teak, which has turned reddish brown under the baptism of years. The interior decoration of the villa resembles a luxurious cruise ship, and the elements of the cruise ship can be seen inadvertently, such as the circular holes on the stairs, the fleet or seascape wood carvings, the compass ceiling, the sea**** and kelp patterns on the floor, and so on.
Turning to the outside, in addition to the main buildings No. 1 and No. 2, the villa is also connected to the annex buildings, which are high and low, rising and falling, and the shape changes irregularly. People have to be amazed and admire the designer's whimsy. With such a large volume, no wonder we get dizzy. The whole floor is ocher red, made of refractory bricks, embedded with colored Taishan facing bricks, which is unique to the world of fairy tales. There are two sloping roofs of different heights on the top of the main building. The sloping roof on the east side is nearly 20 meters high, with arched oriel windows on it, and relief decorations on the top of the spire and the oriel windows; 25 meters with a steep roof. The doors and windows are arched, and the frames protrude from the wall. There are small minarets on the top and corners of the buildings, which are beautiful in shape. Norwegian-style minarets, Gothic-style spires, and this kind of tall and steep roof are the designs for resisting cold wind and reducing snow on the roof in the Nordic region. It's mysterious and wonderful!
The garden is on the south side of the main building, surrounded by colored tiles. The bronze horse at the entrance of the garden is shaped by Mahler to commemorate his beloved mount. It is the racehorse on which Mahler made his fortune. This horse often wins races and is known as the "good luck horse" in Shanghai at that time. A small ditch surrounds the garden, and a small stone bridge is placed in the east and west. There are rare flowers and trees such as cypress and cedar in the garden, and a neatly trimmed green lawn in the middle. There is a beautiful small flower house against the wall next to the creek. The sign on it says "Painted Boat", which is the name of a Chinese garden. I guess it used to be a place for gardeners' tools, but now it is a small private room. Across the lawn, opposite the main building is the flower viewing room. The room was originally equipped with heating equipment. The interior is exquisitely carved and the floor is covered with colorful tiles. It is now used as a lobby of the hotel.

wifi:

info:Superior Room (2 beds)

rating:5
posted:Posted November 27, 2021
msg:The Mahler Villa, also known as Mahler House, has a rich history. The British Jew Mahler built this unique Norwegian house based on the style seen in his daughter‚Äôs dream. It was built for 9 years and was completed in 1936. Soon after the villa was built, it encountered the War of Resistance Against Japan. After the Japanese entered the concession in 1941, the Mahler family was rushed to a concentration camp. The villa became a club for the Japanese army. In order to avoid the war, Mahler left China and stayed here. The "dream castle" that can't be taken away. After the victory of the Anti-Japanese War, it became an organ of the Kuomintang, and later the office of the Municipal Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Committee, and now it has become a villa hotel where the people can spend money. After more than eighty years, only cats have been frequent visitors in Mahler Villa.
Closer to home, when we checked in, a big apricot tree in the garden just started to turn yellow, and it should be beautiful in a few days. Whether from the large floor-to-ceiling glass on the first floor or the windows on the second and third floors, you can see the beautiful scenery, and little sisters. Gathered at the Mahler Villa and spent a happily and happily day and night.
üöó Transportation: convenient
üßπ Hygiene: clean, duvet and pillow are very comfortable
üçÉ Environment: very elegant. There are real stories in old buildings
üîîService: Very good
